<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 7.01&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Regulation FD Disclosure.</u></font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On
March&nbsp;22, 2010, Target Corporation, through its wholly-owned subsidiaries,
Target Receivables Corporation and Target National Bank, delivered certain
monthly reports relating to the Floating Rate Class&nbsp;A Asset Backed Notes, Series&nbsp;2005-1,
and the Subordinated Interests, Series&nbsp;2005-1, issued by the Target Credit
Card Owner Trust 2005-1 to the Trustee. These reports are being furnished as
exhibits to this report.</font></p>

<div>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Exhibit 20.1</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">MONTHLY SERVICER&#146;S CERTIFICATE</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TARGET NATIONAL BANK</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TARGET CREDIT CARD MASTER TRUST</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SERIES 2005-1</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The undersigned, a duly authorized
representative of Target National Bank, as Servicer (&#147;Target National Bank&#148; or
the &#147;Servicer&#148;), pursuant to the Amended and Restated Pooling and Servicing
Agreement, dated as of April&nbsp;28, 2000, as amended by Amendment No.&nbsp;1
thereto, dated as of August&nbsp;22, 2001 (as may be amended, supplemented or
otherwise modified, the &#147;Agreement&#148;), as supplemented by the Series&nbsp;2005-1
Supplement (as may be amended, from time to time, the
&#147;Series&nbsp;Supplement&#148;), dated as of November&nbsp;9, 2005, by and among
Target National Bank, Target Receivables Corporation and Wells Fargo Bank,
National Association, does hereby certify as follows:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Capitalized terms used in this
Certificate have their respective meanings as set forth in the Agreement or the
Series&nbsp;Supplement, as applicable.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Target National Bank is, as of the
date hereof, the Servicer under the Agreement.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The undersigned is a Servicing
Officer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This certificate relates to the
Distribution Date occuring on March&nbsp;25, 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of the date hereof, to the best
knowledge of the undersigned, the Servicer has performed in all material
respects all its obligations under the Agreement through the Monthly Period
preceding such Distribution Date.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of the date hereof, to the best
knowledge of the undersigned, no Early Amortization Commencement Date occurred
on or prior to such Distribution Date.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The aggregate amount of Collections
processed for the preceding Monthly Period was equal to $970,872,409.27.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The aggregate amount of Collections
of Finance Charge Receivables (including Discounted Receivables) for the
preceding Monthly Period was equal to $155,370,129.06.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The aggregate amount of Collections
of Principal Receivables for the preceding Monthly Period was equal to
$815,502,280.21.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The aggregate amount of the
Defaulted Amount for the preceding Monthly Period was equal to $96,980,041.88.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The aggregate amount of Recoveries
for the preceding Monthly Period was equal to $10,168,450.81.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Portfolio Yield for the
preceding Monthly Period was equal to 10.81%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Base Rate for the preceding
Monthly Period was equal to 2.23%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.35in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">14.</font><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The aggregate amount of Receivables
